### Post by yabbadabbadont on 2007-10-28
tautology



When Rav created the game the first time round, he spelled out that you had to use two adjacent letters from the word, neither of which could be either the first or last letter.  (which meant that all words must be at least four letters long)  Things were going well until a newly promoted moderator (we assume.  there were several new ones at that time)   went on a thread merging spree and merged all four (or was it 3?) of the different word games into one thread.  This screwed up all of them.  Once they created the games forum, Rav started the ones that hadn't survived back up again.  That ends todays history lesson.  :D

---

### Post by xyz on 2007-10-28
> **yabbadabbadont said:**
> tautology



When Rav created the game the first time round, he spelled out that you had to use two adjacent letters from the word, neither of which could be either the first or last letter.  (which meant that all words must be at least four letters long)  Things were going well until a newly promoted moderator (we assume.  there were several new ones at that time)   went on a thread merging spree and merged all four (or was it 3?) of the different word games into one thread.  This screwed up all of them.  Once they created the games forum, Rav started the ones that hadn't survived back up again.  That ends todays history lesson.  :D

I have now been clearly informed. :wink:

tour

### Post by p_quarles on 2008-01-05
> **xyz said:**
> kenyan

Can you please explain what Tandoori and Dolphin have to do together? Thnx.
If you read the first post in this thread, you'll see that the basic rule of the game is to post a new word that begins with any two consecutive letters -- other than the first or last -- from the previous word. The word "dolphin", e.g., begins with two letters that occur in the middle of the word "tandoori." 

> **meindian523 said:**
> knickers
nitrogen

Sa[COLOR="Red"]ha[/COLOR]ra -> [COLOR="Red"]ha[/COLOR]

You can't go from Sahara to hectare because there is no 'he' in Sahara.

Sa[COLOR="Red"]ha[/COLOR]ra -> [COLOR="Red"]ha[/COLOR]

I then went:
[COLOR="Red"]ha[/COLOR] -> [COLOR="Red"]ha[/COLOR]rangue

So isn't the word now harangue?

malarkey

@p_quarles: They did a pretty good job clearing it when I was there many years ago.  Which reminds me, there was an empty lot with concrete cars (sculptures I guess) right next to the hotel in which I stayed.  I remember it mostly because, as I was walking back to the hotel from the bank at 3:00AM, one of the guys with me pointed them out to me.  "Look at all those small dogs running around over there." ### Post by lukjad on 2008-10-16
mistress
An interesting side note is that Mrs should not have a period since it doesn't stand for missus but mistress, the original name for a married woman. This meaning was dropped when the other meaning of mistress came into general use.
